    60	        manager := NewManager[T](svr)
    61

    66	}

    75	        handler, group := SetUpRestHandler(s)

    79	// GetManager returns the resource manager.

    84	func (s *Service) checkServing() error {
    85	        if s.manager == nil || s.manager.srv == nil || !s.manager.srv.IsServing() {
    86	                return errs.ErrNotLeader
    87	        }
    88	        return nil
    89	}

    91	// GetResourceGroup implements ResourceManagerServer.GetResourceGroup.
    92	func (s *Service) GetResourceGroup(_ context.Context, req *rmpb.GetResourceGroupRequest) (*rmpb.GetResourceGroupResponse, error) {
    93	        if err := s.checkServing(); err != nil {
    94	                return nil, err
    95	        }
    96	        rg, err := s.manager.GetResourceGroup(ExtractKeyspaceID(req.GetKeyspaceId()), req.ResourceGroupName, req.WithRuStats)
    97	        if err != nil {
    98	                return nil, err
    99	        }
   100	        if rg == nil {
   101	                return nil, errs.ErrResourceGroupNotExists.FastGenByArgs(req.ResourceGroupName)
   102	        }
   103	        return &rmpb.GetResourceGroupResponse{
   104	                Group: rg.IntoProtoResourceGroup(),
   105	        }, nil
   106	}
   107	
   108	// ListResourceGroups implements ResourceManagerServer.ListResourceGroups.
   109	func (s *Service) ListResourceGroups(_ context.Context, req *rmpb.ListResourceGroupsRequest) (*rmpb.ListResourceGroupsResponse, error) {
   110	        if err := s.checkServing(); err != nil {
   111	                return nil, err
   112	        }
   113	        groups, err := s.manager.GetResourceGroupList(ExtractKeyspaceID(req.GetKeyspaceId()), req.WithRuStats)
   114	        if err != nil {
   115	                return nil, err
   116	        }
   117	        resp := &rmpb.ListResourceGroupsResponse{
   118	                Groups: make([]*rmpb.ResourceGroup, 0, len(groups)),
   119	        }
   120	        for _, group := range groups {
   121	                resp.Groups = append(resp.Groups, group.IntoProtoResourceGroup())
   122	        }
   123	        return resp, nil
   124	}

   162	// AcquireTokenBuckets implements ResourceManagerServer.AcquireTokenBuckets.
   163	func (s *Service) AcquireTokenBuckets(stream rmpb.ResourceManager_AcquireTokenBucketsServer) error {
   164	        for {
   165	                select {
   166	                case <-s.ctx.Done():
   167	                        return errors.New("server closed")
   168	                default:
   169	                }
   170	                request, err := stream.Recv()
   171	                if err == io.EOF {
   172	                        return nil
   173	                }
   174	                failpoint.Inject("acquireFailed", func() {
   175	                        err = errors.New("error")
   176	                })
   177	                if err != nil {
   178	                        return errors.WithStack(err)
   179	                }
   180	                if err := s.checkServing(); err != nil {
   181	                        return err
   182	                }
   183	                var (
   184	                        targetPeriodMs = request.GetTargetRequestPeriodMs()
   185	                        clientUniqueID = request.GetClientUniqueId()
   186	                        resps          = &rmpb.TokenBucketsResponse{}
   187	                        logFields      = make([]zap.Field, 2)
   188	                )
   189	                for _, req := range request.Requests {
   190	                        keyspaceID := ExtractKeyspaceID(req.GetKeyspaceId())
   191	                        resourceGroupName := req.GetResourceGroupName()
   192	                        logFields[0] = zap.Uint32("keyspace-id", keyspaceID)
   193	                        logFields[1] = zap.String("resource-group", resourceGroupName)
   194	                        // Get keyspace resource group manager to apply service limit later.
   195	                        krgm := s.manager.getKeyspaceResourceGroupManager(keyspaceID)
   196	                        if krgm == nil {
   197	                                log.Warn("keyspace resource group manager not found", logFields...)
   198	                                continue
   199	                        }
   200	                        // Get the resource group from manager to acquire token buckets.
   201	                        rg, err := s.manager.GetMutableResourceGroup(keyspaceID, resourceGroupName)
   202	                        if rg == nil {
   203	                                log.Warn("resource group not found", append(logFields, zap.Error(err))...)
   204	                                continue
   205	                        }
   206	                        // Send the consumption to update the metrics.
   207	                        err = s.manager.dispatchConsumption(req)
   208	                        if err != nil {
   209	                                return err
   210	                        }
   211	                        if req.GetIsBackground() {
   212	                                continue
   213	                        }
   214	                        now := time.Now()
   215	                        resp := &rmpb.TokenBucketResponse{
   216	                                ResourceGroupName: rg.Name,
   217	                                KeyspaceId:        &rmpb.KeyspaceIDValue{Value: keyspaceID},
   218	                        }
   219	                        switch rg.Mode {
   220	                        case rmpb.GroupMode_RUMode:
   221	                                var tokens *rmpb.GrantedRUTokenBucket
   222	                                for _, re := range req.GetRuItems().GetRequestRU() {
   223	                                        if re.Type == rmpb.RequestUnitType_RU {
   224	                                                tokens = rg.RequestRU(now, re.Value, targetPeriodMs, clientUniqueID, krgm.getServiceLimiter())
   225	                                        }
   226	                                        if tokens == nil {
   227	                                                continue
   228	                                        }
   229	                                        resp.GrantedRUTokens = append(resp.GrantedRUTokens, tokens)
   230	                                }
   231	                        case rmpb.GroupMode_RawMode:
   232	                                log.Warn("not supports the resource type",
   233	                                        append(logFields, zap.String("mode", rmpb.GroupMode_name[int32(rmpb.GroupMode_RawMode)]))...)
   234	                                continue
   235	                        }
   236	                        log.Debug("finish token request from", logFields...)
   237	                        resps.Responses = append(resps.Responses, resp)
   238	                }
   239	                if err := stream.Send(resps); err != nil {
   240	                        return errors.WithStack(err)
   241	                }
   242	        }
   243	}
   244

    37	const (

    41	        keyspaceResourceGroupSettingPathPrefix            = "resource_group/keyspace/settings/%d"
    42	        controllerConfigPathPrefix                        = "resource_group/controller"
    43	)
    44	
    45	// GroupSettingsPathPrefixBytes is used to watch or get resource groups.
    46	func GroupSettingsPathPrefixBytes(keyspaceID uint32) []byte {
    47	        if keyspaceID == constants.NullKeyspaceID {
    48	                return []byte(groupSettingsPathPrefix)
    49	        }
    50	        return fmt.Appendf(nil, keyspaceResourceGroupSettingPathPrefix, keyspaceID)
    51	}
    52	
    53	// ControllerConfigPathPrefixBytes is used to watch or get controller config.
    54	var ControllerConfigPathPrefixBytes = []byte(controllerConfigPathPrefix)
    55	
    56	// ResourceManagerClient manages resource group info and token request.
    57	type ResourceManagerClient interface {
    58	        ListResourceGroups(ctx context.Context, opts ...GetResourceGroupOption) ([]*rmpb.ResourceGroup, error)
    59	        GetResourceGroup(ctx context.Context, resourceGroupName string, opts ...GetResourceGroupOption) (*rmpb.ResourceGroup, error)
    60	        AddResourceGroup(ctx context.Context, metaGroup *rmpb.ResourceGroup) (string, error)
    61	        ModifyResourceGroup(ctx context.Context, metaGroup *rmpb.ResourceGroup) (string, error)
    62	        DeleteResourceGroup(ctx context.Context, resourceGroupName string) (string, error)
    63	        LoadResourceGroups(ctx context.Context) ([]*rmpb.ResourceGroup, int64, error)
    64	        AcquireTokenBuckets(ctx context.Context, request *rmpb.TokenBucketsRequest) ([]*rmpb.TokenBucketResponse, error)
    65	        Watch(ctx context.Context, key []byte, opts ...opt.MetaStorageOption) (chan []*meta_storagepb.Event, error)
    66	}
    67	
    68	// GetResourceGroupOp represents available options when getting resource group.
    69	type GetResourceGroupOp struct {
    70	        withRUStats bool
    71	}
    72	
    73	// GetResourceGroupOption configures GetResourceGroupOp.
    74	type GetResourceGroupOption func(*GetResourceGroupOp)
    75	
    76	// WithRUStats specifies to return resource group with ru statistics data.
    77	func WithRUStats(op *GetResourceGroupOp) {
    78	        op.withRUStats = true
    79	}
    80	
    81	// resourceManagerClient gets the ResourceManager client of current PD leader.
    82	func (c *innerClient) resourceManagerClient() (rmpb.ResourceManagerClient, error) {
    83	        cc, err := c.getOrCreateGRPCConn()
    84	        if err != nil {
    85	                return nil, err
    86	        }
    87	        return rmpb.NewResourceManagerClient(cc), nil
    88	}
    89	
    90	// ListResourceGroups loads and returns all metadata of resource groups.
    91	func (c *client) ListResourceGroups(ctx context.Context, ops ...GetResourceGroupOption) ([]*rmpb.ResourceGroup, error) {
    92	        cc, err := c.inner.resourceManagerClient()
    93	        if err != nil {
    94	                return nil, err
    95	        }
    96	        getOp := &GetResourceGroupOp{}
    97	        for _, op := range ops {
    98	                op(getOp)
    99	        }
   100	        req := &rmpb.ListResourceGroupsRequest{
   101	                WithRuStats: getOp.withRUStats,
   102	                KeyspaceId: &rmpb.KeyspaceIDValue{
   103	                        Value: c.inner.keyspaceID,
   104	                },
   105	        }
   106	        resp, err := cc.ListResourceGroups(ctx, req)
   107	        if err != nil {
   108	                c.inner.gRPCErrorHandler(err)
   109	                return nil, errs.ErrClientListResourceGroup.FastGenByArgs(err.Error())
   110	        }
   111	        resErr := resp.GetError()
   112	        if resErr != nil {
   113	                return nil, errs.ErrClientListResourceGroup.FastGenByArgs(resErr.Message)
   114	        }
   115	        return resp.GetGroups(), nil
   116	}
   117	
   118	// GetResourceGroup implements the ResourceManagerClient interface.
   119	func (c *client) GetResourceGroup(ctx context.Context, resourceGroupName string, ops ...GetResourceGroupOption) (*rmpb.ResourceGroup, error) {
   120	        cc, err := c.inner.resourceManagerClient()
   121	        if err != nil {
   122	                return nil, err
   123	        }
   124	        getOp := &GetResourceGroupOp{}
   125	        for _, op := range ops {
   126	                op(getOp)
   127	        }
   128	        req := &rmpb.GetResourceGroupRequest{
   129	                ResourceGroupName: resourceGroupName,
   130	                WithRuStats:       getOp.withRUStats,
   131	                KeyspaceId: &rmpb.KeyspaceIDValue{
   132	                        Value: c.inner.keyspaceID,
   133	                },
   134	        }
   135	        resp, err := cc.GetResourceGroup(ctx, req)
   136	        if err != nil {
   137	                c.inner.gRPCErrorHandler(err)
   138	                return nil, &errs.ErrClientGetResourceGroup{ResourceGroupName: resourceGroupName, Cause: err.Error()}
   139	        }
   140	        resErr := resp.GetError()
   141	        if resErr != nil {
   142	                return nil, &errs.ErrClientGetResourceGroup{ResourceGroupName: resourceGroupName, Cause: resErr.Message}
   143	        }
   144	        return resp.GetGroup(), nil
   145	}

   147	// AddResourceGroup implements the ResourceManagerClient interface.
   148	func (c *client) AddResourceGroup(ctx context.Context, metaGroup *rmpb.ResourceGroup) (string, error) {
   149	        return c.putResourceGroup(ctx, metaGroup, add)
   150	}
   151	
   152	// ModifyResourceGroup implements the ResourceManagerClient interface.
   153	func (c *client) ModifyResourceGroup(ctx context.Context, metaGroup *rmpb.ResourceGroup) (string, error) {
   154	        return c.putResourceGroup(ctx, metaGroup, modify)
   155	}
   156	
   157	func (c *client) putResourceGroup(ctx context.Context, metaGroup *rmpb.ResourceGroup, typ actionType) (string, error) {
   158	        cc, err := c.inner.resourceManagerClient()
   159	        if err != nil {
   160	                return "", err
   161	        }
   162	        req := &rmpb.PutResourceGroupRequest{
   163	                Group: metaGroup,
   164	        }
   165	        var resp *rmpb.PutResourceGroupResponse
   166	        switch typ {
   167	        case add:
   168	                resp, err = cc.AddResourceGroup(ctx, req)
   169	        case modify:
   170	                resp, err = cc.ModifyResourceGroup(ctx, req)
   171	        }
   172	        if err != nil {
   173	                c.inner.gRPCErrorHandler(err)
   174	                return "", err
   175	        }
   176	        resErr := resp.GetError()
   177	        if resErr != nil {
   178	                return "", errors.Errorf("[resource_manager] %s", resErr.Message)
   179	        }
   180	        return resp.GetBody(), nil
   181	}
   182	
   183	// DeleteResourceGroup implements the ResourceManagerClient interface.
   184	func (c *client) DeleteResourceGroup(ctx context.Context, resourceGroupName string) (string, error) {
   185	        cc, err := c.inner.resourceManagerClient()
   186	        if err != nil {
   187	                return "", err
   188	        }
   189	        req := &rmpb.DeleteResourceGroupRequest{
   190	                ResourceGroupName: resourceGroupName,
   191	                KeyspaceId: &rmpb.KeyspaceIDValue{
   192	                        Value: c.inner.keyspaceID,
   193	                },
   194	        }
   195	        resp, err := cc.DeleteResourceGroup(ctx, req)
   196	        if err != nil {
   197	                c.inner.gRPCErrorHandler(err)
   198	                return "", err
   199	        }
   200	        resErr := resp.GetError()
   201	        if resErr != nil {
   202	                return "", errors.Errorf("[resource_manager] %s", resErr.Message)
   203	        }
   204	        return resp.GetBody(), nil
   205	}
   206	
   207	// LoadResourceGroups implements the ResourceManagerClient interface.
   208	func (c *client) LoadResourceGroups(ctx context.Context) ([]*rmpb.ResourceGroup, int64, error) {
   209	        prefix := GroupSettingsPathPrefixBytes(c.inner.keyspaceID)
   210	        resp, err := c.Get(ctx, prefix, opt.WithPrefix())
   211	        if err != nil {
   212	                return nil, 0, err
   213	        }
   214	        if resp.Header.Error != nil {
   215	                return nil, resp.Header.Revision, errors.New(resp.Header.Error.Message)
   216	        }
   217	        groups := make([]*rmpb.ResourceGroup, 0, len(resp.Kvs))
   218	        for _, item := range resp.Kvs {
   219	                group := &rmpb.ResourceGroup{}
   220	                if err := proto.Unmarshal(item.Value, group); err != nil {
   221	                        continue
   222	                }
   223	                groups = append(groups, group)
   224	        }
   225	        return groups, resp.Header.Revision, nil
   226	}
   227	
   228	// AcquireTokenBuckets implements the ResourceManagerClient interface.
   229	func (c *client) AcquireTokenBuckets(ctx context.Context, request *rmpb.TokenBucketsRequest) ([]*rmpb.TokenBucketResponse, error) {
   230	        req := &tokenRequest{
   231	                done:       make(chan error, 1),
   232	                requestCtx: ctx,
   233	                clientCtx:  c.inner.ctx,
   234	                Request:    request,
   235	        }
   236	        c.inner.tokenDispatcher.tokenBatchController.tokenRequestCh <- req
   237	        grantedTokens, err := req.wait()
   238	        if err != nil {
   239	                return nil, err
   240	        }
   241	        return grantedTokens, err
   242	}
   243	
   244	type tokenRequest struct {
   245	        clientCtx    context.Context
   246	        requestCtx   context.Context
   247	        done         chan error
   248	        Request      *rmpb.TokenBucketsRequest
   249	        TokenBuckets []*rmpb.TokenBucketResponse
   250	}
   251	
   252	func (req *tokenRequest) wait() (tokenBuckets []*rmpb.TokenBucketResponse, err error) {
   253	        select {
   254	        case err = <-req.done:
   255	                err = errors.WithStack(err)
   256	                if err != nil {
   257	                        return nil, err
   258	                }
   259	                tokenBuckets = req.TokenBuckets
   260	                return
   261	        case <-req.requestCtx.Done():
   262	                return nil, errors.WithStack(req.requestCtx.Err())
   263	        case <-req.clientCtx.Done():
   264	                return nil, errors.WithStack(req.clientCtx.Err())
   265	        }
   266	}
   267	
   268	type tokenBatchController struct {
   269	        tokenRequestCh chan *tokenRequest
   270	}
   271	
   272	func newTokenBatchController(tokenRequestCh chan *tokenRequest) *tokenBatchController {
   273	        return &tokenBatchController{
   274	                tokenRequestCh: tokenRequestCh,
   275	        }
   276	}
   277	
   278	type tokenDispatcher struct {
   279	        dispatcherCancel     context.CancelFunc
   280	        tokenBatchController *tokenBatchController
   281	}
   282	
   283	type resourceManagerConnectionContext struct {
   284	        stream rmpb.ResourceManager_AcquireTokenBucketsClient
   285	        ctx    context.Context
   286	        cancel context.CancelFunc
   287	}
   288	
   289	func (cc *resourceManagerConnectionContext) reset() {
   290	        cc.stream = nil
   291	        if cc.cancel != nil {
   292	                cc.cancel()
   293	        }
   294	}
   295	
   296	func (c *innerClient) createTokenDispatcher() {
   297	        dispatcherCtx, dispatcherCancel := context.WithCancel(c.ctx)
   298	        dispatcher := &tokenDispatcher{
   299	                dispatcherCancel: dispatcherCancel,
   300	                tokenBatchController: newTokenBatchController(
   301	                        make(chan *tokenRequest, 1)),
   302	        }
   303	        c.wg.Add(1)
   304	        go c.handleResourceTokenDispatcher(dispatcherCtx, dispatcher.tokenBatchController)
   305	        c.tokenDispatcher = dispatcher
   306	}
   307	
   308	func (c *innerClient) handleResourceTokenDispatcher(dispatcherCtx context.Context, tbc *tokenBatchController) {
   309	        defer func() {
   310	                log.Info("[resource manager] exit resource token dispatcher")
   311	                c.wg.Done()
   312	        }()
   313	        var (
   314	                connection   resourceManagerConnectionContext
   315	                firstRequest *tokenRequest
   316	                stream       rmpb.ResourceManager_AcquireTokenBucketsClient
   317	                streamCtx    context.Context
   318	                toReconnect  bool
   319	                err          error
   320	        )
   321	        if err = c.tryResourceManagerConnect(dispatcherCtx, &connection); err != nil {
   322	                log.Warn("[resource_manager] get token stream error", zap.Error(err))
   323	        }
   324	        for {
   325	                // Fetch the request from the channel.
   326	                select {
   327	                case <-dispatcherCtx.Done():
   328	                        return
   329	                case firstRequest = <-tbc.tokenRequestCh:
   330	                }
   331	                // Try to get a stream connection.
   332	                stream, streamCtx = connection.stream, connection.ctx
   333	                select {
   334	                case <-c.updateTokenConnectionCh:
   335	                        toReconnect = true
   336	                default:
   337	                        toReconnect = stream == nil
   338	                }
   339	                // If the stream is nil or the leader has changed, try to reconnect.
   340	                if toReconnect {
   341	                        connection.reset()
   342	                        if err := c.tryResourceManagerConnect(dispatcherCtx, &connection); err != nil {
   343	                                log.Error("[resource_manager] try to connect token leader failed", errs.ZapError(err))
   344	                        }
   345	                        log.Info("[resource_manager] token leader may change, try to reconnect the stream")
   346	                        stream, streamCtx = connection.stream, connection.ctx
   347	                }
   348	                // If the stream is still nil, return an error.
   349	                if stream == nil {
   350	                        firstRequest.done <- errors.Errorf("failed to get the stream connection")
   351	                        c.serviceDiscovery.ScheduleCheckMemberChanged()
   352	                        connection.reset()
   353	                        continue
   354	                }
   355	                select {
   356	                case <-streamCtx.Done():
   357	                        connection.reset()
   358	                        log.Info("[resource_manager] token stream is canceled")
   359	                        continue
   360	                default:
   361	                }
   362	                if err = c.processTokenRequests(stream, firstRequest); err != nil {
   363	                        c.serviceDiscovery.ScheduleCheckMemberChanged()
   364	                        connection.reset()
   365	                        log.Info("[resource_manager] token request error", zap.Error(err))
   366	                }
   367	        }
   368	}
   369	
   370	func (c *innerClient) processTokenRequests(stream rmpb.ResourceManager_AcquireTokenBucketsClient, t *tokenRequest) error {
   371	        req := t.Request
   372	        if err := stream.Send(req); err != nil {
   373	                err = errors.WithStack(err)
   374	                t.done <- err
   375	                return err
   376	        }
   377	        resp, err := stream.Recv()
   378	        if err != nil {
   379	                c.gRPCErrorHandler(err)
   380	                err = errors.WithStack(err)
   381	                t.done <- err
   382	                return err
   383	        }
   384	        if resp.GetError() != nil {
   385	                return errors.Errorf("[resource_manager] %s", resp.GetError().Message)
   386	        }
   387	        t.TokenBuckets = resp.GetResponses()
   388	        t.done <- nil
   389	        return nil
   390	}
   391	
   392	func (c *innerClient) tryResourceManagerConnect(ctx context.Context, connection *resourceManagerConnectionContext) error {
   393	        var (
   394	                err    error
   395	                stream rmpb.ResourceManager_AcquireTokenBucketsClient
   396	        )
   397	        ticker := time.NewTicker(constants.RetryInterval)
   398	        defer ticker.Stop()
   399	        for range constants.MaxRetryTimes {
   400	                cc, err := c.resourceManagerClient()
   401	                if err != nil {
   402	                        continue
   403	                }
   404	                cctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(ctx)
   405	                stream, err = cc.AcquireTokenBuckets(cctx)
   406	                if err == nil && stream != nil {
   407	                        connection.cancel = cancel
   408	                        connection.ctx = cctx
   409	                        connection.stream = stream
   410	                        return nil
   411	                }
   412	                cancel()
   413	                select {
   414	                case <-ctx.Done():
   415	                        return err
   416	                case <-ticker.C:
   417	                }
   418	        }
   419	        return err
   420	}
   421	
   422	func (tbc *tokenBatchController) revokePendingTokenRequest(err error) {
   423	        for range len(tbc.tokenRequestCh) {
   424	                req := <-tbc.tokenRequestCh
   425	                req.done <- err
   426	        }
   427	}
   428

    15	package server

    17	import (
    18	        "math"
    19	        "time"
    20	
    21	        "github.com/gogo/protobuf/proto"
    22	        "go.uber.org/zap"
    23	
    24	        rmpb "github.com/pingcap/kvproto/pkg/resource_manager"
    25	        "github.com/pingcap/log"
    26	)
    27	
    28	const (
    29	        defaultRefillRate         = 10000
    30	        defaultModeratedBurstRate = 10000
    31	        defaultInitialTokens      = 10 * 10000
    32	        defaultReserveRatio       = 0.5
    33	        defaultLoanCoefficient    = 2
    34	        maxAssignTokens           = math.MaxFloat64 / 1024 // assume max client connect is 1024
    35	        slotExpireTimeout         = 10 * time.Minute
    36	)
    37	
    38	type burstableMode int
    39	
    40	const (
    41	        limited        burstableMode = iota // burstlimit is greater than 0
    42	        rateControlled                      // burstlimit is 0
    43	        unlimited                           // burstlimit is -1
    44	        moderated                           // burstlimit is -2
    45	)
    46	
    47	func getBurstableMode(settings *rmpb.TokenLimitSettings) burstableMode {
    48	        if settings == nil {
    49	                return limited
    50	        }
    51	        // BurstLimit is used as below:
    52	        //   - If b == 0, that means the limiter is unlimited capacity. default use in resource controller (burst with a rate within an unlimited capacity).
    53	        //   - If b == -1, that means the limiter is unlimited capacity and fillrate(r) is ignored, can be seen as r == Inf (burst within an unlimited capacity).
    54	        //   - If b == -2, that means the limiter is limited capacity and fillrate(r) is ignored, can be seen as r == defaultBurstLimitFactor * fillrate (burst within a limited capacity).
    55	        //   - If b > 0, that means the limiter is limited capacity.
    56	        burst := settings.GetBurstLimit()
    57	        switch {
    58	        case burst == -1:
    59	                return unlimited
    60	        case burst == -2:
    61	                return moderated
    62	        case burst == 0:
    63	                return rateControlled
    64	        case burst > 0:
    65	                return limited
    66	        default:
    67	                log.Warn("invalid burst limit, fallback to limited mode",
    68	                        zap.Int64("burst-limit", burst))
    69	                return limited
    70	        }
    71	}
    72	
    73	// GroupTokenBucket is a token bucket for a resource group.
    74	// Now we don't save consumption in `GroupTokenBucket`, only statistics it in prometheus.
    75	type GroupTokenBucket struct {
    76	        // Settings is the setting of TokenBucket.
    77	        // MaxTokens limits the number of tokens that can be accumulated
    78	        Settings              *rmpb.TokenLimitSettings `json:"settings,omitempty"`
    79	        GroupTokenBucketState `json:"state,omitempty"`
    80	}
    81	
    82	func (gtb *GroupTokenBucket) getFillRateSetting() float64 {
    83	        return float64(gtb.Settings.GetFillRate())
    84	}
    85	
    86	func (gtb *GroupTokenBucket) setFillRateSetting(fillRate uint64) {
    87	        gtb.Settings.FillRate = fillRate
    88	}
    89	
    90	func (gtb *GroupTokenBucket) getBurstLimitSetting() int64 {
    91	        return gtb.Settings.GetBurstLimit()
    92	}
    93	
    94	func (gtb *GroupTokenBucket) clone() *GroupTokenBucket {
    95	        if gtb == nil {
    96	                return nil
    97	        }
    98	        var settings *rmpb.TokenLimitSettings
    99	        if gtb.Settings != nil {
   100	                settings = proto.Clone(gtb.Settings).(*rmpb.TokenLimitSettings)
   101	        }
   102	        stateClone := *gtb.GroupTokenBucketState.clone()
   103	        return &GroupTokenBucket{
   104	                Settings:              settings,
   105	                GroupTokenBucketState: stateClone,
   106	        }
   107	}
   108	
   109	func (gtb *GroupTokenBucket) setState(state *GroupTokenBucketState) {
   110	        gtb.Tokens = state.Tokens
   111	        gtb.LastUpdate = state.LastUpdate
   112	        gtb.Initialized = state.Initialized
   113	}
   114	
   115	// tokenSlot is used to split a token bucket into multiple slots to
   116	// server different clients within the same resource group.
   117	type tokenSlot struct {
   118	        fillRate   uint64
   119	        burstLimit int64
   120	        // requireTokensSum is the number of tokens required.
   121	        requireTokensSum float64
   122	        // tokenCapacity is the number of tokens in the slot.
   123	        tokenCapacity     float64
   124	        lastTokenCapacity float64
   125	        lastReqTime       time.Time
   126	}
   127	
   128	// GroupTokenBucketState is the running state of TokenBucket.
   129	type GroupTokenBucketState struct {
   130	        Tokens float64 `json:"tokens,omitempty"`
   131	        // ClientUniqueID -> TokenSlot
   132	        tokenSlots                 map[uint64]*tokenSlot
   133	        clientConsumptionTokensSum float64
   134	        // Used to store tokens in the token slot that exceed burst limits,
   135	        // ensuring that these tokens are not lost but are reintroduced into
   136	        // token calculation during the next update.
   137	        lastBurstTokens float64
   138	        // Used to store tokens that exceed the service limit,
   139	        // ensuring that these tokens are not lost but are reintroduced into
   140	        // token calculation during the next update.
   141	        lastLimitedTokens float64
   142	
   143	        LastUpdate  *time.Time `json:"last_update,omitempty"`
   144	        Initialized bool       `json:"initialized"`
   145	        // settingChanged is used to avoid that the number of tokens returned is jitter because of changing fill rate.
   146	        settingChanged      bool
   147	        lastCheckExpireSlot time.Time
   148	}
   149	
   150	func (gts *GroupTokenBucketState) clone() *GroupTokenBucketState {
   151	        var tokenSlots map[uint64]*tokenSlot
   152	        if gts.tokenSlots != nil {
   153	                tokenSlots = make(map[uint64]*tokenSlot)
   154	                for id, tokens := range gts.tokenSlots {
   155	                        tokenSlots[id] = tokens
   156	                }
   157	        }
   158	
   159	        var lastUpdate *time.Time
   160	        if gts.LastUpdate != nil {
   161	                newLastUpdate := *gts.LastUpdate
   162	                lastUpdate = &newLastUpdate
   163	        }
   164	        return &GroupTokenBucketState{
   165	                Tokens:                     gts.Tokens,
   166	                LastUpdate:                 lastUpdate,
   167	                Initialized:                gts.Initialized,
   168	                tokenSlots:                 tokenSlots,
   169	                clientConsumptionTokensSum: gts.clientConsumptionTokensSum,
   170	                lastCheckExpireSlot:        gts.lastCheckExpireSlot,
   171	        }
   172	}
   173	
   174	func (gts *GroupTokenBucketState) resetLoan() {
   175	        gts.settingChanged = false
   176	        gts.Tokens = 0
   177	        gts.clientConsumptionTokensSum = 0
   178	        evenRatio := 1.0
   179	        if l := len(gts.tokenSlots); l > 0 {
   180	                evenRatio = 1 / float64(l)
   181	        }
   182	
   183	        evenTokens := gts.Tokens * evenRatio
   184	        for _, slot := range gts.tokenSlots {
   185	                slot.requireTokensSum = 0
   186	                slot.tokenCapacity = evenTokens
   187	                slot.lastTokenCapacity = evenTokens
   188	        }
   189	}
   190	
   191	func (gtb *GroupTokenBucket) balanceSlotTokens(
   192	        clientUniqueID uint64,
   193	        requiredToken, elapseTokens float64,
   194	) {
   195	        now := time.Now()
   196	        slot, exist := gtb.tokenSlots[clientUniqueID]
   197	        if !exist {
   198	                // Only slots that require a positive number will be considered alive,
   199	                // but still need to allocate the elapsed tokens as well.
   200	                if requiredToken != 0 {
   201	                        slot = &tokenSlot{lastReqTime: now}
   202	                        gtb.tokenSlots[clientUniqueID] = slot
   203	                        gtb.clientConsumptionTokensSum = 0
   204	                }
   205	        } else {
   206	                slot.lastReqTime = now
   207	                if gtb.clientConsumptionTokensSum >= maxAssignTokens {
   208	                        gtb.clientConsumptionTokensSum = 0
   209	                }
   210	                // Clean up slot that required 0.
   211	                if requiredToken == 0 {
   212	                        delete(gtb.tokenSlots, clientUniqueID)
   213	                        gtb.clientConsumptionTokensSum = 0
   214	                }
   215	        }
   216	
   217	        if time.Since(gtb.lastCheckExpireSlot) >= slotExpireTimeout {
   218	                gtb.lastCheckExpireSlot = now
   219	                for clientUniqueID, slot := range gtb.tokenSlots {
   220	                        if time.Since(slot.lastReqTime) >= slotExpireTimeout {
   221	                                delete(gtb.tokenSlots, clientUniqueID)
   222	                                log.Info("delete resource group slot because expire",
   223	                                        zap.Time("last-req-time", slot.lastReqTime),
   224	                                        zap.Duration("expire-timeout", slotExpireTimeout),
   225	                                        zap.Uint64("del-client-id", clientUniqueID),
   226	                                        zap.Int("len", len(gtb.tokenSlots)))
   227	                        }
   228	                }
   229	        }
   230	        if len(gtb.tokenSlots) == 0 {
   231	                return
   232	        }
   233	        evenRatio := 1 / float64(len(gtb.tokenSlots))
   234	        if mode := getBurstableMode(gtb.Settings); mode == rateControlled || mode == unlimited {
   235	                for _, slot := range gtb.tokenSlots {
   236	                        slot.fillRate = uint64(gtb.getFillRateSetting() * evenRatio)
   237	                        slot.burstLimit = gtb.getBurstLimitSetting()
   238	                }
   239	                return
   240	        }
   241	
   242	        for _, slot := range gtb.tokenSlots {
   243	                if gtb.clientConsumptionTokensSum == 0 || len(gtb.tokenSlots) == 1 {
   244	                        // Need to make each slot even.
   245	                        slot.tokenCapacity = evenRatio * gtb.Tokens
   246	                        slot.lastTokenCapacity = evenRatio * gtb.Tokens
   247	                        slot.requireTokensSum = 0
   248	                        gtb.clientConsumptionTokensSum = 0
   249	
   250	                        slot.fillRate, slot.burstLimit = gtb.calcRateAndBurstLimit(evenRatio)
   251	                } else {
   252	                        // In order to have fewer tokens available to clients that are currently consuming more.
   253	                        // We have the following formula:
   254	                        //              client1: (1 - a/N + 1/N) * 1/N
   255	                        //              client2: (1 - b/N + 1/N) * 1/N
   256	                        //              ...
   257	                        //              clientN: (1 - n/N + 1/N) * 1/N
   258	                        // Sum is:
   259	                        //              (N - (a+b+...+n)/N +1) * 1/N => (N - 1 + 1) * 1/N => 1
   260	                        ratio := (1 - slot.requireTokensSum/gtb.clientConsumptionTokensSum + evenRatio) * evenRatio
   261	
   262	                        assignToken := elapseTokens * ratio
   263	                        fillRate, burstLimit := gtb.calcRateAndBurstLimit(ratio)
   264	
   265	                        // Need to reserve burst limit to next balance.
   266	                        if burstLimit > 0 && slot.tokenCapacity > float64(burstLimit) {
   267	                                reservedTokens := slot.tokenCapacity - float64(burstLimit)
   268	                                gtb.lastBurstTokens += reservedTokens
   269	                                gtb.Tokens -= reservedTokens
   270	                                assignToken -= reservedTokens
   271	                        }
   272	
   273	                        slot.tokenCapacity += assignToken
   274	                        slot.lastTokenCapacity += assignToken
   275	                        slot.fillRate = fillRate
   276	                        slot.burstLimit = burstLimit
   277	                }
   278	        }
   279	        if requiredToken != 0 {
   280	                // Only slots that require a positive number will be considered alive.
   281	                slot.requireTokensSum += requiredToken
   282	                gtb.clientConsumptionTokensSum += requiredToken
   283	        }
   284	}
   285	
   286	func (gtb *GroupTokenBucket) calcRateAndBurstLimit(ratio float64) (fillRate uint64, burstLimit int64) {
   287	        if getBurstableMode(gtb.Settings) == moderated {
   288	                fillRate = uint64(math.Min(gtb.getFillRateSetting()+defaultModeratedBurstRate, unlimitedRate) * ratio)
   289	                burstLimit = int64(fillRate)
   290	                return
   291	        }
   292	        fillRate = uint64(gtb.getFillRateSetting() * ratio)
   293	        burstLimit = int64(float64(gtb.getBurstLimitSetting()) * ratio)
   294	        return
   295	}
   296	
   297	// NewGroupTokenBucket returns a new GroupTokenBucket
   298	func NewGroupTokenBucket(tokenBucket *rmpb.TokenBucket) *GroupTokenBucket {
   299	        if tokenBucket == nil || tokenBucket.Settings == nil {
   300	                return &GroupTokenBucket{}
   301	        }
   302	        return &GroupTokenBucket{
   303	                Settings: tokenBucket.GetSettings(),
   304	                GroupTokenBucketState: GroupTokenBucketState{
   305	                        Tokens:     tokenBucket.GetTokens(),
   306	                        tokenSlots: make(map[uint64]*tokenSlot),
   307	                },
   308	        }
   309	}
   310	
   311	// GetTokenBucket returns the grpc protoc struct of GroupTokenBucket.
   312	func (gtb *GroupTokenBucket) GetTokenBucket() *rmpb.TokenBucket {
   313	        if gtb.Settings == nil {
   314	                return nil
   315	        }
   316	        return &rmpb.TokenBucket{
   317	                Settings: gtb.Settings,
   318	                Tokens:   gtb.Tokens,
   319	        }
   320	}
   321	
   322	// patch patches the token bucket settings.
   323	func (gtb *GroupTokenBucket) patch(tb *rmpb.TokenBucket) {
   324	        if tb == nil {
   325	                return
   326	        }
   327	        if setting := proto.Clone(tb.GetSettings()).(*rmpb.TokenLimitSettings); setting != nil {
   328	                gtb.Settings = setting
   329	                gtb.settingChanged = true
   330	        }
   331	
   332	        // The settings in token is delta of the last update and now.
   333	        gtb.Tokens += tb.GetTokens()
   334	}
   335	
   336	// init initializes the group token bucket.
   337	func (gtb *GroupTokenBucket) init(now time.Time, clientID uint64) {
   338	        if gtb.getFillRateSetting() == 0 {
   339	                gtb.setFillRateSetting(defaultRefillRate)
   340	        }
   341	        if gtb.Tokens < defaultInitialTokens && gtb.getBurstLimitSetting() > 0 {
   342	                gtb.Tokens = defaultInitialTokens
   343	        }
   344	        // init slot
   345	        gtb.tokenSlots[clientID] = &tokenSlot{
   346	                // Copy settings to avoid modifying the original settings.
   347	                fillRate:          uint64(gtb.getFillRateSetting()),
   348	                burstLimit:        gtb.getBurstLimitSetting(),
   349	                tokenCapacity:     gtb.Tokens,
   350	                lastTokenCapacity: gtb.Tokens,
   351	        }
   352	        gtb.LastUpdate = &now
   353	        gtb.lastCheckExpireSlot = now
   354	        gtb.Initialized = true
   355	}
   356	
   357	// updateTokens updates the tokens and settings.
   358	func (gtb *GroupTokenBucket) updateTokens(now time.Time, burstLimit int64, clientUniqueID uint64, requiredToken float64) {
   359	        var elapseTokens float64
   360	        if !gtb.Initialized {
   361	                gtb.init(now, clientUniqueID)
   362	        } else if burst := float64(burstLimit); burst > 0 {
   363	                if delta := now.Sub(*gtb.LastUpdate); delta > 0 {
   364	                        elapseTokens = gtb.getFillRateSetting()*delta.Seconds() + gtb.lastBurstTokens + gtb.lastLimitedTokens
   365	                        gtb.lastBurstTokens = 0
   366	                        gtb.lastLimitedTokens = 0
   367	                        gtb.Tokens += elapseTokens
   368	                }
   369	                if gtb.Tokens > burst {
   370	                        elapseTokens -= gtb.Tokens - burst
   371	                        gtb.Tokens = burst
   372	                }
   373	        }
   374	        gtb.LastUpdate = &now
   375	        // Reloan when setting changed
   376	        if gtb.settingChanged && gtb.Tokens <= 0 {
   377	                elapseTokens = 0
   378	                gtb.resetLoan()
   379	        }
   380	        // Balance each slots.
   381	        gtb.balanceSlotTokens(clientUniqueID, requiredToken, elapseTokens)
   382	}
   383	
   384	// request requests tokens from the corresponding slot.
   385	func (gtb *GroupTokenBucket) request(now time.Time,
   386	        requiredToken float64,
   387	        targetPeriodMs, clientUniqueID uint64,
   388	) (*rmpb.TokenBucket, int64) {
   389	        burstLimit := gtb.getBurstLimitSetting()
   390	        gtb.updateTokens(now, burstLimit, clientUniqueID, requiredToken)
   391	        slot, ok := gtb.tokenSlots[clientUniqueID]
   392	        if !ok {
   393	                return &rmpb.TokenBucket{Settings: &rmpb.TokenLimitSettings{BurstLimit: burstLimit}}, 0
   394	        }
   395	        res, trickleDuration := slot.assignSlotTokens(requiredToken, targetPeriodMs)
   396	        // Update bucket to record all tokens.
   397	        gtb.Tokens -= slot.lastTokenCapacity - slot.tokenCapacity
   398	        slot.lastTokenCapacity = slot.tokenCapacity
   399	
   400	        return res, trickleDuration
   401	}
   402	
   403	func (ts *tokenSlot) assignSlotTokens(requiredToken float64, targetPeriodMs uint64) (*rmpb.TokenBucket, int64) {
   404	        var res rmpb.TokenBucket
   405	        burstLimit := ts.burstLimit
   406	        res.Settings = &rmpb.TokenLimitSettings{BurstLimit: burstLimit}
   407	        if getBurstableMode(res.Settings) == unlimited {
   408	                res.Tokens = requiredToken
   409	                return &res, 0
   410	        }
   411	        // FillRate is used for the token server unavailable in abnormal situation.
   412	        if requiredToken <= 0 {
   413	                return &res, 0
   414	        }
   415	        // If the current tokens can directly meet the requirement, returns the need token.
   416	        if ts.tokenCapacity >= requiredToken {
   417	                ts.tokenCapacity -= requiredToken
   418	                // granted the total request tokens
   419	                res.Tokens = requiredToken
   420	                return &res, 0
   421	        }
   422	
   423	        // Firstly allocate the remaining tokens
   424	        var grantedTokens float64
   425	        hasRemaining := false
   426	        if ts.tokenCapacity > 0 {
   427	                grantedTokens = ts.tokenCapacity
   428	                requiredToken -= grantedTokens
   429	                ts.tokenCapacity = 0
   430	                hasRemaining = true
   431	        }
   432	
   433	        var (
   434	                targetPeriodTime    = time.Duration(targetPeriodMs) * time.Millisecond
   435	                targetPeriodTimeSec = targetPeriodTime.Seconds()
   436	                trickleTime         = 0.
   437	                fillRate            = ts.fillRate
   438	        )
   439	
   440	        loanCoefficient := defaultLoanCoefficient
   441	        // When BurstLimit less or equal FillRate, the server does not accumulate a significant number of tokens.
   442	        // So we don't need to smooth the token allocation speed.
   443	        if burstLimit > 0 && burstLimit <= int64(fillRate) {
   444	                loanCoefficient = 1
   445	        }
   446	        // When there are loan, the allotment will match the fill rate.
   447	        // We will have k threshold, beyond which the token allocation will be a minimum.
   448	        // The threshold unit is `fill rate * target period`.
   449	        //               |
   450	        // k*fill_rate   |* * * * * *     *
   451	        //               |                        *
   452	        //     ***       |                                 *
   453	        //               |                                           *
   454	        //               |                                                     *
   455	        //   fill_rate   |                                                                 *
   456	        // reserve_rate  |                                                                              *
   457	        //               |
   458	        // grant_rate 0  ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   459	        //         loan      ***    k*period_token    (k+k-1)*period_token    ***      (k+k+1...+1)*period_token
   460	
   461	        // loanCoefficient is relative to the capacity of load RUs.
   462	        // It's like a buffer to slow down the client consumption. the buffer capacity is `(1 + 2 ... +loanCoefficient) * fillRate * targetPeriodTimeSec`.
   463	        // Details see test case `TestGroupTokenBucketRequestLoop`.
   464	
   465	        p := make([]float64, loanCoefficient)
   466	        p[0] = float64(loanCoefficient) * float64(fillRate) * targetPeriodTimeSec
   467	        for i := 1; i < loanCoefficient; i++ {
   468	                p[i] = float64(loanCoefficient-i)*float64(fillRate)*targetPeriodTimeSec + p[i-1]
   469	        }
   470	        for i := 0; i < loanCoefficient && requiredToken > 0 && trickleTime < <response clipped><NOTE>To save on context only part of this file has been shown to you. You should retry this tool after you have searched inside the file with `grep -n` in order to find the line numbers of what you are looking for.</NOTE>

message TokenBucketRequest {
    message RequestRU {
        repeated RequestUnitItem request_r_u = 1;
    }
    message RequestRawResource {
        repeated RawResourceItem request_raw_resource = 1;
    }

    string resource_group_name = 1;
    oneof request {
        // RU mode, group settings with WRU/RRU etc resource abstract unit.
        RequestRU ru_items = 2;
        // Raw mode, group settings with CPU/IO etc resource unit.
        RequestRawResource raw_resource_items = 3;
    }
    // Aggregate statistics in group level.
    Consumption consumption_since_last_request = 4;
    // label background request.
    bool is_background = 5;
    bool is_tiflash = 6;
    // There're two cases for this field:
    //   - If the keyspace ID is not set, it means this may be a message from an older version.
    //     To maintain compatibility, we will treat it as a null keyspace ID, which is uint32.Max.
    //   - If the keyspace ID is set to a valid value, it will try to request the token bucket from
    //     the resource group within the given keyspace ID.
    KeyspaceIDValue keyspace_id = 7;
}

  Error error = 1;
  repeated TokenBucketResponse responses = 2;

  1378	
  1379	func (gc *groupCostController) calcRequest(counter *tokenCounter) float64 {
  1380	        // `needTokensAmplification` is used to properly amplify a need. The reason is that in the current implementation,
  1381	        // the token returned from the server determines the average consumption speed.
  1382	        // Therefore, when the fillrate of resource group increases, `needTokensAmplification` can enable the client to obtain more tokens.
  1383	        value := counter.avgRUPerSec * gc.run.targetPeriod.Seconds() * needTokensAmplification
  1384	        value -= counter.limiter.AvailableTokens(gc.run.now)
  1385	        if value < 0 {
  1386	                value = 0
  1387	        }
  1388	        return value
  1389	}

Now I understand the issue! Looking at the code, I can see that:

1. In `/testbed/pkg/mcs/resourcemanager/server/grpc_service.go` at line 190, the code tries to extract the keyspace ID from the `TokenBucketRequest`:
   ```go
   keyspaceID := ExtractKeyspaceID(req.GetKeyspaceId())
   ```

2. The `TokenBucketRequest` proto message does have a `keyspace_id` field (field number 7), as confirmed by the proto definition.

3. However, when the client creates a `TokenBucketRequest` in the `collectRequestAndConsumption` method in `/testbed/client/resource_group/controller/controller.go`, it does NOT set the `KeyspaceId` field in the request:
   ```go
   req := &rmpb.TokenBucketRequest{
       ResourceGroupName: gc.name,
   }
   ```

The issue is that the client is not setting the `KeyspaceId` field when creating the `TokenBucketRequest`, which means when the server tries to extract it using `req.GetKeyspaceId()`, it gets `nil`, and then `ExtractKeyspaceID` returns `constant.NullKeyspaceID` (which is 0).

The solution is to modify the client code to set the `KeyspaceId` field when creating the `TokenBucketRequest`. Let me check how the client gets the keyspace ID:

Now I understand the issue! Looking at the PR description and the code analysis:

1. The problem is in the `TokenBucketRequest` - it doesn't have the `keyspace_id` field set when it should.
2. In the gRPC service at line 190 of `/testbed/pkg/mcs/resourcemanager/server/grpc_service.go`, it extracts the keyspace ID from the request, but the request doesn't have this field set.
3. Looking at the client-side code `/testbed/client/resource_group/controller/controller.go`, the `collectRequestAndConsumption` function creates a `TokenBucketRequest` but doesn't set the `KeyspaceId` field.

	"fmt"

)

	req := &rmpb.TokenBucketRequest{

					Type:  rmpb.RequestUnitType_RU,

2026-01-08 15:54:02,059 - INFO - swea-agent - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I understand the complete picture. The issue is that the `TokenBucketRequest` objects created by the client don't have the `KeyspaceId` field set, but the server expects this field to be present.

Looking at the code flow:
1. The client creates `TokenBucketRequest` objects in `collectRequestAndConsumption`
2. These requests are bundled into a `TokenBucketsRequest` that's sent to the server
3. The server tries to extract the keyspace ID from each individual `TokenBucketRequest` but finds it's nil

The solution is to modify the code to set the `KeyspaceId` field when creating `TokenBucketRequest` objects. The keyspace ID is available in the `ResourceGroupsController` but needs to be passed down to the `groupCostController` or accessed during request creation.

Let me implement the fix:

🎬 ACTION

   536	// Do not delete the resource group immediately to prevent from interrupting the ongoing request,
   537	// mark it as tombstone and create a default resource group controller for it.
   538	func (c *ResourceGroupsController) tombstoneGroupCostController(name string) {
   539	        _, ok := c.loadGroupController(name)
   540	        if !ok {
   541	                return
   542	        }
   543	        // The default resource group controller should never be deleted.
   544	        if name == defaultResourceGroupName {
   545	                return
   546	        }
   547	        // Try to get the default group meta first.
   548	        defaultGC, err := c.tryGetResourceGroupController(c.loopCtx, defaultResourceGroupName, false)
   549	        if err != nil || defaultGC == nil {
   550	                log.Warn("[resource group controller] get default resource group meta for tombstone failed",
   551	                        zap.String("name", name), zap.Error(err))
   552	                // Directly delete the resource group controller if the default group is not available.
   553	                c.groupsController.Delete(name)
   554	                return
   555	        }
   556	        // Create a default resource group controller for the tombstone resource group independently.
   557	        gc, err := newGroupCostController(defaultGC.getMeta(), c.ruConfig, c.lowTokenNotifyChan, c.tokenBucketUpdateChan)

   559	                log.Warn("[resource group controller] create default resource group cost controller for tombstone failed",

2026-01-08 15:56:16,030 - INFO - swea-agent - 💭 THOUGHT
Based on my investigation, I have identified the issue. The problem is that when the client creates a `TokenBucketRequest` in the `collectRequestAndConsumption` method, it doesn't set the `KeyspaceId` field. This field is needed by the server to properly identify which keyspace the resource group belongs to for proper routing and metrics tracking.

Let me fix this issue:



🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor str_replace /testbed/client/resource_group/controller/controller.go   --old_str 'func (gc *groupCostController) collectRequestAndConsumption(selectTyp selectType) *rmpb.TokenBucketRequest {
	req := &rmpb.TokenBucketRequest{
		ResourceGroupName: gc.name,
	}
	// collect request resource
	selected := gc.run.requestInProgress
	failpoint.Inject("triggerUpdate", func() {
		selected = true
	})
	switch gc.mode {
	case rmpb.GroupMode_RawMode:
		requests := make([]*rmpb.RawResourceItem, 0, len(requestResourceLimitTypeList))
		for typ, counter := range gc.run.resourceTokens {
			switch selectTyp {
			case periodicReport:
				selected = selected || gc.shouldReportConsumption()
				fallthrough
			case lowToken:
				if counter.limiter.IsLowTokens() {
					selected = true
				}
			}
			request := &rmpb.RawResourceItem{
				Type:  typ,
				Value: gc.calcRequest(counter),
			}
			requests = append(requests, request)
		}
		req.Request = &rmpb.TokenBucketRequest_RawResourceItems{
			RawResourceItems: &rmpb.TokenBucketRequest_RequestRawResource{
				RequestRawResource: requests,
			},
		}
	case rmpb.GroupMode_RUMode:
		requests := make([]*rmpb.RequestUnitItem, 0, len(requestUnitLimitTypeList))
		for typ, counter := range gc.run.requestUnitTokens {
			switch selectTyp {
			case periodicReport:
				selected = selected || gc.shouldReportConsumption()
				failpoint.Inject("triggerPeriodicReport", func(val failpoint.Value) {
					selected = gc.name == val.(string)
				})
				fallthrough
			case lowToken:
				if counter.limiter.IsLowTokens() {
					selected = true
				}
				failpoint.Inject("triggerLowRUReport", func(val failpoint.Value) {
					if selectTyp == lowToken {
						selected = gc.name == val.(string)
					}
				})
			}
			request := &rmpb.RequestUnitItem{
				Type:  typ,
				Value: gc.calcRequest(counter),
			}
			requests = append(requests, request)
		}
		req.Request = &rmpb.TokenBucketRequest_RuItems{
			RuItems: &rmpb.TokenBucketRequest_RequestRU{
				RequestRU: requests,
			},
		}
	}
	if !selected {
		return nil
	}
	req.ConsumptionSinceLastRequest = updateDeltaConsumption(gc.run.lastRequestConsumption, gc.run.consumption)
	gc.run.lastRequestTime = time.Now()
	gc.run.requestInProgress = true
	return req
}' --new_str 'func (gc *groupCostController) collectRequestAndConsumption(selectTyp selectType) *rmpb.TokenBucketRequest {
	req := &rmpb.TokenBucketRequest{
		ResourceGroupName: gc.name,
	}
	// Try to get KeyspaceId from the resource group meta
	if gc.meta != nil && gc.meta.KeyspaceId != nil {
		req.KeyspaceId = gc.meta.KeyspaceId
	}
	// collect request resource
	selected := gc.run.requestInProgress
	failpoint.Inject("triggerUpdate", func() {
		selected = true
	})
	switch gc.mode {
	case rmpb.GroupMode_RawMode:
		requests := make([]*rmpb.RawResourceItem, 0, len(requestResourceLimitTypeList))
		for typ, counter := range gc.run.resourceTokens {
			switch selectTyp {
			case periodicReport:
				selected = selected || gc.shouldReportConsumption()
				fallthrough
			case lowToken:
				if counter.limiter.IsLowTokens() {
					selected = true
				}
			}
			request := &rmpb.RawResourceItem{
				Type:  typ,
				Value: gc.calcRequest(counter),
			}
			requests = append(requests, request)
		}
		req.Request = &rmpb.TokenBucketRequest_RawResourceItems{
			RawResourceItems: &rmpb.TokenBucketRequest_RequestRawResource{
				RequestRawResource: requests,
			},
		}
	case rmpb.GroupMode_RUMode:
		requests := make([]*rmpb.RequestUnitItem, 0, len(requestUnitLimitTypeList))
		for typ, counter := range gc.run.requestUnitTokens {
			switch selectTyp {
			case periodicReport:
				selected = selected || gc.shouldReportConsumption()
				failpoint.Inject("triggerPeriodicReport", func(val failpoint.Value) {
					selected = gc.name == val.(string)
				})
				fallthrough
			case lowToken:
				if counter.limiter.IsLowTokens() {
					selected = true
				}
				failpoint.Inject("triggerLowRUReport", func(val failpoint.Value) {
					if selectTyp == lowToken {
						selected = gc.name == val.(string)
					}
				})
			}
			request := &rmpb.RequestUnitItem{
				Type:  typ,
				Value: gc.calcRequest(counter),
			}
			requests = append(requests, request)
		}
		req.Request = &rmpb.TokenBucketRequest_RuItems{
			RuItems: &rmpb.TokenBucketRequest_RequestRU{
				RequestRU: requests,
			},
		}
	}
	if !selected {
		return nil
	}
	req.ConsumptionSinceLastRequest = updateDeltaConsumption(gc.run.lastRequestConsumption, gc.run.consumption)
	gc.run.lastRequestTime = time.Now()
	gc.run.requestInProgress = true
	return req
}'

import (

)

func main() {
	// Test case 1: TokenBucketRequest without KeyspaceId (old behavior)
	fmt.Println("=== Test Case 1: Old behavior (without KeyspaceId) ===")
	req1 := &rmpb.TokenBucketRequest{
		ResourceGroupName: "test_group",
		Request: &rmpb.TokenBucketRequest_RuItems{
			RuItems: &rmpb.TokenBucketRequest_RequestRU{
				RequestRU: []*rmpb.RequestUnitItem{
					{
						Type:  rmpb.RequestUnitType_RU,
						Value: 1000,
					},
				},
			},
		},
	}
	
	if req1.KeyspaceId == nil {
		fmt.Println("ISSUE CONFIRMED: TokenBucketRequest.KeyspaceId is nil")
		fmt.Println("This will result in empty string after getKeyspaceNameByID")
	} else {
		fmt.Printf("KeyspaceId is set: %v\n", req1.KeyspaceId)
	}
	
	// Test case 2: TokenBucketRequest with KeyspaceId (with our fix)
	fmt.Println("\n=== Test Case 2: With fix (with KeyspaceId) ===")

						Value: 1000,
					},
				},
			},
		},
	}

	} else {
		fmt.Println("UNEXPECTED: KeyspaceId should be nil")
	}

func (gc *groupCostController) modifyMeta(newMeta *rmpb.ResourceGroup) {
	gc.metaLock.Lock()
	defer gc.metaLock.Unlock()
	gc.meta = newMeta
}
